# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Setting all sources
which are inside the set
to zero  ^fJ2v75Pn

setting     to zero ^OVFhYwH7

Due to SUPERPOSITION method,
the original voltage       will be
equal to  ^JuoXs3pV

Using KVL: ^ckdueTEV

*Reminder <KVL>
Sum of voltage in a circuit
must be zero. ^ljklt9ED

All value can be known
- V_oc: Open circuit voltage
- R_eq: Equivalence Resistance
    with all sources in circuit off ^Wkz94wty
